Its base combines mono-dispersed, plant-derived glycogen, availability-enhancing Myristoyl Nonapeptide-3 and cross-linked hyaluronic acid.\n\n PRO-HEALTH TECHNOLOGIES\n\n1.0% Pure Undiluted Copper Tripeptide-1 (GHK-Cu) + 1.0% Pure Undiluted Tripeptide-1 (GHK)\nCAIS 3 1:1 supplies 1% pure GHK peptide (Tripeptide-1), alongside 1% Copper Tripeptide-1 (GHK-Cu). Both GHK and GHK-Cu are found in nature and originally isolated from human plasma. The concentration of these peptides in human plasma continues to drop with aging past late teenage years.The natural role of these peptides as found in the human body includes activation of a wide range of skin health functions, including healing, immune function, collagen synthesis, fibroblast production and anti-inflammatory responses, while pure GHK offers strong pro-collagen support.\n\nThe 2% concentration of GHK and GHK-Cu in CAIS 3 1:1 aims to target visible signs of skin aging, including textural irregularities, uneven tone, visibly enlarged pores and a general lack of healthy radiance normally present in younger skin. In short, the skin will look healthier with visible improvements with continued use.\n\nPRO-COLLAGEN TECHNOLOGIES\n\n9.0% Pure Undiluted Tripeptide-29\nThis amino acid sequence of Glycine-Proline-Hydroxyproline supports healthy collagen and works synergistically with GHK and GHK-Cu in this function.\n\n4.0% Complex of Acetyl Tetrapeptide-2 and Trifluroacetyl Tripeptide-2\nWhile pro-collagen peptides broadly focus on collagen quantity, these advanced peptide technologies support healthy collagen quality and assembly for skin that looks firmer and more evenly modelled.\n\n\nINTEGRITY AND DELIVERY TECHNOLOGIES\n\n0.10% Pure Mono-Dispersed Plant Glycogen\nGlycogen is generally extracted from animal sources as a poly-dispersion. This advanced 100% plant-based mono-dispersed glycogen acts like hard spheres that protect the formulation peptides but break upon application for optimal dermal exposure.\n\n9% Complex of Myristoyl Nonapeptide-3\nThis lipo-oligopeptide supports healthy skin renewal which is essential for maximising skin availability of technologies in this formulation and those used in any subsequent treatments.\n\nHyaluronic Acid Crosspolymer\nA unique cross-linked non-animal form of hyaluronic acid helps with delivery of water and water-soluble actives through its non-equilibrium gel structure.\n\n"
